2023 : SD 29.8 shows that it was struck (tinabĕh). The fact that taṅguli gĕṇḍiṅ, t. garantaṅ and t. kĕtur appear to be interchangeable may suggest that gĕṇḍiṅ, garantaṅ (garantuṅ) and kĕtur were similar. Cf also manuk gĕṇḍiṅ, m. garantuṅ, m. titiran, m. kĕtur, and mṛdaṅga as suitable waṅsalan for gĕṇḍiṅ (NR 31.18) |SD 29.8 shows that it was struck (tinabĕh). The fact that taṅguli gĕṇḍiṅ, t. garantaṅ and t. kĕtur appear to be interchangeable may suggest that gĕṇḍiṅ, garantaṅ (garantuṅ) and kĕtur were similar. Cf also manuk gĕṇḍiṅ, m. garantuṅ, m. titiran, m. kĕtur, and mṛdaṅga as suitable waṅsalan for gĕṇḍiṅ (NR 31.18).  gĕṇḍiṅ, gaṇḍiṅ
